GT Equivalence Verification (CRK21)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A*exp(-c1*_s*t) + c2*_q*A*log(c3*t + c4)
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function (for all real \(t,A\)):
\[
F(t,A)=0.08820105614498638\,A\log(0.4381050266935539\,t+1)\;-\;0.9112380846295999\,A\,e^{-0.08901020540483869\,t}.
\]
Key structural facts about GT:

- It is **linear in \(A\)** (every term is \(A\times\)something in \(t\)).
- It contains a **logarithm in \(t\)**: \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\) with \(\alpha\neq 0\).
- It contains a **decaying exponential in \(t\)** multiplied by \(A\): \(A e^{-\beta t}\) with \(\beta\neq 0\).
- No \(|A|\), no \(A^2\), no Max, no rational-in-\(A\), etc.

So any matching candidate must be able (by parameter choice) to produce exactly “\(A\log(\alpha t+1)\) + \(A e^{-\beta t}\)” and must not introduce any nonlinearity in \(A\) or extra \(t\)-dependences.

---

### 1.
\(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 \max(0,-A+c3)+ c4 + c5|A| + c6 e^{c7 t}|A|^{c8}\)

Has Max in \(A\), \(|A|\), and extra constant term. You can zero some terms, but you cannot create \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). **No match**.

### 2.
\(A c0 + A^{c1} c2 e^{c3 t} + c4\)

Only polynomial-in-\(A\) times exponential-in-\(t\) plus constants. No log-in-\(t\). Also constant term \(c4\) must be 0, and linear-in-\(A\) forces \(c1=1\), still no log. **No match**.

### 3.
\(A c0 + A^{c1} c2 e^{c3 t} + c4 t e^{c5 t}\)

Has a term independent of \(A\) unless \(c4=0\). Still no \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). **No match**.

### 4.
\(A c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A c3\max(0,c4+t)+ c5 e^{c6 t}+ c7 e^{c8\max(0,c9+t)}\)

Piecewise Max in \(t\) and extra exponentials not multiplied by \(A\). Can’t become \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). **No match**.

### 5.
\(\frac{c0|A|^{c1}}{c2+t}+\frac{c3 e^{c4|A|}}{c2+t}+\frac{c5 t |A|^{c1}}{c2+t}\)

Rational in \(t\), nonlinear in \(A\), no log-in-\(t\) of affine. **No match**.

### 6.
\(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2|A| + c3 + c4|A| + c5 \frac{|A|^{c6}}{c7+|A|^{c6}}\)

Nonlinear in \(A\) and no \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). **No match**.

### 7.
\(A^2 c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A c3 + A c4|A| + A \frac{c5}{c6|A|+1}+ c7 + c8|A|\)

Has \(A^2\), \(|A|\), rational in \(|A|\). GT is linear in \(A\) and has log-in-\(t\). **No match**.

### 8.
Similar issues: \(A^2\), \(|A|\), saturating fraction. No log-in-\(t\). **No match**.

### 9.
\(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 (t+1)^{c3} + c4 + c5|A| + c6 e^{c7|A|^{c8}}\)

Has power \((t+1)^{c3}\) not \(\log(\alpha t+1)\); also \(|A|\) terms. **No match**.

### 10.
\(A c0 e^{c1 t} + c2 + c3|A|^{c4}\)

No log-in-\(t\); also nonlinearity in \(A\) unless \(c3=0\). Then only exponential term remains, missing log term. **No match**.

### 11.
Contains \(A^2\), \((t+1)^{-5}\), and weird \(e^{c8/|A|^{1/5}}\). Not GT. **No match**.

### 12.
\(A c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A c3 + c4 + c5 t e^{c6 t}\)

Even if \(c4=c5=0\), it’s \(A(\text{constant}+\text{exp})\), no log. **No match**.

### 13.
Has \(A^3, A^2\), etc. Not linear in \(A\). **No match**.

### 14.
Has \(|A|\) and \(\sin(\log(\cdot))\) in \(A\), not log in \(t\). **No match**.

### 15.
\(A c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + c3 e^{c4 t}\)

To avoid the last term (not multiplied by \(A\)), need \(c3=0\). Then no log term. **No match**.

### 16.
\(A c0 e^{c1 t} + c2 + c3|A| + c4 e^{A c5 + c6 t}\)

Has \(e^{A c5}\) dependence unless \(c4=0\). Then no log term. **No match**.

### 17.
\(A c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + c3 t e^{c4 t}\)

Need \(c3=0\) to remove non-\(A\) term; then no log. **No match**.

### 18.
\(A^2 c0 + A c1 + A \frac{c2}{A+c3} + A c4 e^{c5 t} + c6 e^{c7 t}\)

Has \(A^2\), rational in \(A\), and an exponential not multiplied by \(A\). No log-in-\(t\). **No match**.

### 19.
Has \((t+1)^{-5}\), \(|A|\), and \(e^{e^{t}}\). Not GT. **No match**.

### 20.
\(A c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + c3 e^{c4 t} + c5 e^{c6 t}\log(A c7+1)\)

Log is in \(A\), not in \(t\). Also extra non-\(A\) exponential unless \(c3=0\). Still cannot produce \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). **No match**.

### 21.
Has \(|A|\) and rational in \(|A|\). No log-in-\(t\). **No match**.

### 22.
Has \((t+1)^{c3}\) and \(e^{A\cdot e^{t}}\). Not GT. **No match**.

### 23.
Has \(A^2\), sine in \(t\), linear-in-\(t\) terms. No log. **No match**.

### 24.
\(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 + c3 + c4 \log(c5 e^{A^{c6}c7}+1)\)

Log is in \(A\), not \(t\). Also constant term \(c3\). Cannot become \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). **No match**.

### 25.
\(A^2 c0 + A c1 + A c2 e^{c3 t} + c4 t e^{c5 t}\)

Has \(A^2\) and non-\(A\) term unless \(c4=0\). Still no log. **No match**.

### 26.
Has \(A^3, A^2\), Max in \(A\), \(|A|\). Not GT. **No match**.

### 27.

### 28.
\(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 t + A \frac{c3}{A+c4} + c5\)

Contains \(A t\) (linear in \(t\), not log), rational in \(A\), and constant \(c5\). No way to get \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). **No match**.

### 29.
\(A^2 c0 + A c1 + A^{c2} c3 e^{c4 t} + c5 \frac{t}{c6+t^2}\)

Has \(A^2\) and a non-\(A\) rational-in-\(t\) term. No log. **No match**.

### 30.
Has \(A^2\) and \((t+1)^{-5}\) and weird \(A\)-dependent exponential. Not GT. **No match**.

### 31.
\(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2|A| + A \frac{c3}{c4+t} + c5 + c6|A|\)

Nonlinear in \(A\) and rational in \(t\), not log. **No match**.

### 32.
\(A^2 c0 + A c1 + A c2 e^{c3 t} + A c4 + c5 e^{c6 t}\)

Has \(A^2\) and an exponential not multiplied by \(A\) unless \(c5=0\). Still no log. **No match**.

### 33.
Has \(A^2\) and \((t+1)^{c4}\) not log. **No match**.

### 34.
Has \(A^2\) and \((t+1)^{-5}\). No log. **No match**.

### 35.
\(A^2 c0 + A c1 + (c2+c3)t + c4 + c5 e^{c6 t}\log(c7|A|+1)\)

Log is in \(A\), plus \(A^2\), plus linear \(t\) term. Not GT. **No match**.

### 36.
\(A c0 + c1 e^{c2 t} + c3 + c4 t^{c5}|A|^{c6}\)

Has non-\(A\) exponential and constant; also \(|A|\) power term. No \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). **No match**.

### 37.
Has \(A^2\) and \(e^{c5|A|}\). Not GT. **No match**.

### 38.
Has \(A^2\), \(|A|\), and rational in \(A\). Not GT. **No match**.

Log is in \(A\), not \(t\). Also constant term. **No match**.

### 40.
\(A c0 + A c1 (c2+t)^{c3} + c4 e^{c5 t} + c6 e^{c7 t}\sin(c8 t+c9)\)

Power in \(t\) not log; extra non-\(A\) terms. **No match**.

### 41.
Has \(A^2\), \(|A|\), and \(e^{t}|A|\). Not GT. **No match**.

Even setting \(c0=c4=0\), it’s \(A(\text{exp}+\text{const})\) with no log. **No match**.

None of the candidates contains (or can be parameter-specialized to contain) the essential \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\) term while also matching the linear-in-\(A\) structure and the single \(A e^{-\beta t}\) term without introducing forbidden extra dependencies.

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK21)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A*exp(-c1*_s*t) + c2*_q*A*log(c3*t + c4)
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT: 0.08820105614498638*A*log(0.4381050266935539*t + 1) - 0.9112380846295999*A*exp(-0.08901020540483869*t)**

Key observations about the GT:
- It's a function of A and t
- It has two terms, both linear in A
- One term is `A*exp(-αt)` (exponential decay in t)
- The other is `A*log(βt + 1)` (logarithmic growth in t)
- There are NO terms independent of A (no constant offset)
- There are NO terms with A², A³, |A|, etc.

For A ≥ 0 (domain constraint), |A| = A and A*|A| = A².

So the GT = A*(c_exp*exp(-αt) + c_log*log(βt+1)), which is strictly linear in A.

Let me check each candidate for the ability to match this structure. I need:
1. All terms not proportional to A must vanish
2. The A-dependent part must contain exactly exp(negative*t) and log(linear_in_t + const) basis functions

For candidates with |A| terms: since A ≥ 0, |A| = A, so c*|A| = c*A (fine).
For A*|A| = A² terms or A² terms: these are quadratic in A and cannot match (unless coefficient = 0).

Let me systematically check which candidates can zero out non-matching terms and retain the needed basis functions.

The GT has two basis functions in t (for each multiplied by A):
1. exp(-0.089*t)
2. log(0.438*t + 1)

**No candidate contains a log(c*t + c) term** except candidates involving `log(c*exp(...)+1)` or `log(c*|A|+1)` or similar.

Let me check candidates with log terms:
- **Candidate 20**: has `log(A*c7 + 1)` - this is log in A, not log in t
- **Candidate 24**: has `log(c5*exp(A^c6*c7) + 1)` - not log in t
- **Candidate 35**: has `exp(c6*t)*log(c7*|A| + 1)` - log in A, not t
- **Candidate 39**: has `log(c5*exp(c6*|A|) + 1)` - log in A

**None of the candidates contain log(t) or log(c*t + c) as a basis function.**

The GT requires `A*log(βt + 1)` which is a logarithmic function of t. Since log is linearly independent from polynomials, exponentials, rational functions, power functions, trigonometric functions, etc., **no candidate can match the GT** unless it contains a log(t+...) term.

Let me double-check candidates with power-law terms like `(t+1)^c` which could approximate but never exactly equal log:
- Candidates 9, 22, 33, 40 have `(t+1)^c` or `(c+t)^c` terms. But `(t+1)^c` is a power function and is NOT equivalent to `log(βt+1)` for any constant c. These are linearly independent basis functions.

No candidate contains the required `log(linear_in_t)` basis function.

Therefore, **no candidate matches**.
